Le Meridien Powerlong is located in Qibao Town, Minhang District. It is also a resort hotel that is very suitable for checking in on weekends and visiting the ancient town. It is only a ten-minute walk to Qibao Old Street. There are Powerlong shopping malls and Vanke shopping malls next to it. It is very convenient to eat. There are very design works of art everywhere on the first floor of the hotel.

The room design is a combination of marble and metal, very modern, with a slightly frigid feeling, I like it very much; when I checked in, I told the front desk that I like to collect room cards, and the manager on duty, Xiaokang, specially helped me choose two different styles for me. Me, the service was great, and the breakfast was pretty good.

Coordinates: No. 3199, Caobao Road, Minhang District, Shanghai
